## 中文 🇨🇳

### CVE 漏洞库 (NVD)

#### 1. CVE-1999-0095 (N/A)

**CVE/编号**: CVE-1999-0095 [NVD]
**严重程度**: N/A | CVSS: 10.0


**漏洞描述**:
The debug command in Sendmail is enabled, allowing attackers to execute commands as root.

**应对措施 / 缓解方案**:
Refer to vendor security advisory for patch and mitigation guidance.

**参考链接**:
- http://seclists.org/fulldisclosure/2019/Jun/16
- http://www.openwall.com/lists/oss-security/2019/06/05/4
- http://www.openwall.com/lists/oss-security/2019/06/06/1
- http://www.osvdb.org/195
- http://www.securityfocus.com/bid/1

> 📎 来源 / Source: http://seclists.org/fulldisclosure/2019/Jun/16

#### 3. CVE-1999-1471 (N/A)

**CVE/编号**: CVE-1999-1471 [NVD]
**严重程度**: N/A | CVSS: 7.2


**漏洞描述**:
Buffer overflow in passwd in BSD based operating systems 4.3 and earlier allows local users to gain root privileges by specifying a long shell or GECOS field.

**应对措施 / 缓解方案**:
Refer to vendor security advisory for patch and mitigation guidance.

**参考链接**:

#### 7. CVE-1999-0084 (HIGH)

**CVE/编号**: CVE-1999-0084 [NVD]
**严重程度**: HIGH | CVSS: 8.4
CWE: CWE-269

**漏洞描述**:
Certain NFS servers allow users to use mknod to gain privileges by creating a writable kmem device and setting the UID to 0.

**应对措施 / 缓解方案**:
Refer to vendor security advisory for patch and mitigation guidance.

**参考链接**:
- https://exchange.xforce.ibmcloud.com/vulnerabilities/78
- https://exchange.xforce.ibmcloud.com/vulnerabilities/78

> 📎 来源 / Source: https://exchange.xforce.ibmcloud.com/vulnerabilities/78

## English 🇺🇸
**Network Security Vulnerability Knowledge Base**

Auto-updated hourly from NVD, Exploit-DB, GitHub Security Advisories, CISA KEV. Covers CVEs, public exploits (0-Day), and mitigation guidance. Deduplicated and incrementally maintained.

### CVE Database (NVD)

#### 1. CVE-1999-0095 (N/A)

**CVE/ID**: CVE-1999-0095 [NVD]
**Severity**: N/A | CVSS: 10.0


**Description**:
The debug command in Sendmail is enabled, allowing attackers to execute commands as root.

**Mitigation / Countermeasure**:
Refer to vendor security advisory for patch and mitigation guidance.

**References**:
- http://seclists.org/fulldisclosure/2019/Jun/16
- http://www.openwall.com/lists/oss-security/2019/06/05/4
